```mermaid
sequenceDiagram

    Shell->>EnvVars: source _local_set_env_vars.sh

    Shell->>VirtualEnv: source env/bin/activate
    VirtualEnv-->>Shell: Virtual environment activated
    Shell->>Luigi: setsid luigid --background --logdir /var/log/luigi
    Luigi-->>Shell: Daemon started in background
```
